        <div className="bg-[#004b23] text-white p-4 flex justify-between items-center">
          <h2 className="font-bold text-lg flex items-center"><FileText className="mr-2"/> Entrada de Serviço - {vtrDisplay}</h2>
          <div className="flex space-x-3">
            {isDev && (
              <button onClick={() => { if(window.confirm('Apagar Serviço?')) onDelete(data.id) }} className="hover:bg-red-600 bg-red-500 p-1.5 rounded transition shadow-sm text-white" title="Apagar Registro"><Trash2 size={18}/></button>
            )}
            <button onClick={onClose} className="hover:bg-green-800 p-1.5 rounded transition"><XCircle size={24}/></button>
          </div>
        </div>
        
        <div className="p-6 overflow-y-auto flex-1 space-y-6 text-sm">
          
          <div className="bg-blue-50 p-4 rounded-lg border border-blue-200">
             <h3 className="font-bold text-blue-900 mb-2 uppercase border-b border-blue-200 pb-1">Composição da Equipe</h3>
             <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 gap-2">
                {(data.equipe || []).map((eq, i) => (
                  <div key={i} className="bg-white p-2 rounded border border-blue-100 flex justify-between items-center">
                    <div>
                      <span className="text-[10px] text-blue-600 font-bold block">{eq.funcao}</span>
                      <span className="font-bold text-gray-800 text-xs">{eq.posto} {eq.nome}</span>
                    </div>
                    <span className="text-[10px] text-gray-500 font-mono">Mat: {eq.matricula}</span>
                  </div>
                ))}
             </div>
             {(data.trocaRegistrada || getServiceAuditLines(data).length > 0) && (
                <div className="mt-3 p-2 bg-orange-100 text-orange-800 text-xs rounded font-bold border border-orange-300">
                  <AlertTriangle size={14} className="inline mr-1 mb-0.5"/> 
                  Auditoria: {((data.auditoriaLinhas && data.auditoriaLinhas.join(' | ')) || getServiceAuditLines(data).join(' | ')) || data.conflitoAudit || 'Comandante requisitou PMs de outro serviço ativo.'}
                </div>
             )}
          </div>

          <div className="grid grid-cols-2 md:grid-cols-4 gap-4 bg-gray-50 p-4 rounded-lg border">
            <div><span className="block text-xs text-gray-500 uppercase">Data/Registro</span><strong className="text-gray-800">{data.date ? new Date(data.date).toLocaleString() : '--'}</strong></div>
            <div><span className="block text-xs text-gray-500 uppercase">Modalidade</span><strong className="text-gray-800">{data.modalidade}</strong></div>
            <div><span className="block text-xs text-gray-500 uppercase">OPM</span><strong className="text-gray-800">{data.opm}</strong></div>
            <div><span className="block text-xs text-gray-500 uppercase">Rádio HT</span><strong className="text-gray-800">{data.ht || 'N/I'}</strong></div>
            
            <div className="md:col-span-2"><span className="block text-xs text-gray-500 uppercase">Área de Atuação</span><strong className="text-gray-800">{data.areaAtuacao}</strong></div>
            <div><span className="block text-xs text-gray-500 uppercase">Turno / Tipo</span><strong className="text-gray-800">{data.turno} - {data.tipoServico}</strong></div>
            <div><span className="block text-xs text-gray-500 uppercase">Horário</span><strong className="text-blue-700 bg-blue-100 px-2 rounded">{data.horaInicial} às {data.horaFinal}</strong></div>
            
            {data.modalidade !== 'POSTO FIXO' && data.modalidade !== 'A PÉ' && (
              <>
                <div className="md:col-span-2"><span className="block text-xs text-gray-500 uppercase">Veículo(s)</span><strong className="text-gray-800">{vtrDisplay}</strong></div>
                <div><span className="block text-xs text-gray-500 uppercase">KM Atual</span><strong className="text-gray-800">{data.kmAtual}</strong></div>
                <div><span className="block text-xs text-gray-500 uppercase">Troca de Óleo?</span><strong className="text-gray-800">{data.trocaOleo} (Próx: {data.kmProxima})</strong></div>
              </>
            )}
          </div>

          {data.modalidade !== 'POSTO FIXO' && data.modalidade !== 'A PÉ' && (
            <div>
              <h3 className="font-bold text-lg border-b pb-1 mb-4 text-gray-800">Situação da Inspeção Veicular</h3>
              {!temItens ? (
                <div className="bg-gray-50 text-gray-800 p-4 rounded border border-gray-200">
                  <Info className="inline mr-2"/> Nenhum item inspecionado.
                </div>
              ) : (
                <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 gap-4">
                  {Object.entries(categoriasModal).map(([catName, catItems]) => {
                    const itensNaCategoria = catItems.filter(item => data.itens && data.itens[item]);
                    if (itensNaCategoria.length === 0) return null;
                    return (
                      <div key={catName} className="bg-white border border-gray-200 rounded-lg shadow-sm p-4 hover:shadow-md transition">
                        <h4 className="font-bold text-xs text-[#004b23] uppercase mb-3 border-b border-gray-100 pb-2 flex items-center">
                           <Wrench size={14} className="mr-2"/> {catName}
                        </h4>
                        <ul className="space-y-2">
                          {itensNaCategoria.map(item => {
                            const info = data.itens[item];
                            const isAlterado = info?.status === 'Alterado';
                            return (
                              <li key={item} className={`text-xs p-2 rounded flex justify-between items-start ${isAlterado ? 'bg-red-50 text-red-800 border border-red-100' : 'bg-green-50 text-green-800 border border-green-100'}`}>
                                <span className="font-semibold uppercase w-2/3 pr-2 flex items-center">
                                  {isAlterado ? <AlertTriangle size={12} className="mr-1 flex-shrink-0" /> : <CheckCircle size={12} className="mr-1 flex-shrink-0" />}
                                  {item}
                                </span>
                                <span className={`font-bold w-1/3 text-right ${isAlterado ? 'text-red-600' : 'text-green-600'}`}>
                                  {isAlterado ? (info.obs || 'AVARIA') : 'OK'}
                                </span>
                              </li>
                            );
                          })}
                        </ul>
                      </div>
                    );
                  })}
                </div>
              )}
              
              {data.outrasAlteracoes && (
                <div className="mt-4 p-4 bg-orange-50 border border-orange-200 rounded">
                  <strong className="text-orange-800 uppercase text-xs block mb-1">Outras Alterações Constatadas (Texto Livre):</strong>
                  <p className="text-gray-800">{data.outrasAlteracoes}</p>
                </div>
              )}
            </div>
          )}

          {data.fotos && Object.keys(data.fotos).length > 0 && (
            <div>
              <h3 className="font-bold text-lg border-b pb-1 mb-3 text-gray-800">Registro fotográfico de alterações</h3>
              <div className="grid grid-cols-2 md:grid-cols-4 gap-4">
                {Object.keys(data.fotos).map(angle => {
                  const foto = data.fotos[angle];
                  if(!foto) return null;
                  return (
                    <div key={angle} className="border rounded bg-gray-50 overflow-hidden">
                      <img src={foto.url} alt={angle} className="w-full h-32 object-cover" />
                      <div className="p-2 text-center text-xs font-bold text-gray-700 bg-gray-200">{angle}</div>
                    </div>
                  )
                })}
              </div>
            </div>
          )}

          {/* ASSINATURA MODAL */}
          <div className="mt-16 text-center break-inside-avoid">
             <div className="w-64 border-t border-black mx-auto mt-8 pt-2">
                <p className="font-bold uppercase text-sm">{data.equipe?.[0]?.posto} {data.equipe?.[0]?.nomeCompleto || data.equipe?.[0]?.nome || data.userName}</p>
                <p className="text-xs uppercase font-mono">Matrícula: {data.equipe?.[0]?.matricula || data.matricula}</p>
                <p className="text-[10px] font-bold mt-1 text-gray-600 uppercase">Comandante da Equipe</p>
             </div>
          </div>

        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

function OcorrenciaForm({ userData, usersDb, efetivoPlanilha, viaturas, onSave, setView, showToast }) {
  const [step, setStep] = useState(1);
  
  const [formData, setFormData] = useState({
    dataOcorrencia: new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0],
    horaInicial: '', 
    horaFinal: '', 
    turno: '',
    supervisor: '',
    opm: '', 
    opmOutra: '',
    areaAtuacao: '',
    areaSelecionada: '',
    bairrosSelecionados: [],
    areaDigitada: '',
    local: '', 
    coordenadas: '', 
    municipio: '', 
    municipioOutro: '',
    tipoPoliciamento: '', 
    vtrId: '', 
    prefixo: '', 
    ht: '',
    mikeOcorrencia: '',
    equipe: getOccurrenceDefaultTeam('', userData),
    apoio: '', 
    natureza: '', 
    narrativa: '', 
    materialApresentado: '', 
    veiculos: '', 
    armas: '', 
    entorpecentes: '', 
    valores: '',
    envolvidos: '', 
    suspeitos: '', 
    procedimento: '', 
    procedimentoOutro: '',
    anexoProcedimento: null,
    capitulacao: '', 
    situacaoConduzido: 'LIBERADO', 
    situacaoConduzidoOutro: '',
    delegado: '', 
    escrivao: '', 
    comentarios: '',
    anexosGerais: []
  });

  const handleMatriculaChange = (id, val) => {
    let cleanVal = formatMatricula(val); 
    setFormData(prev => {
      const newEquipe = prev.equipe.map(m => {
        if (m.id === id) {
          let novoNome = ''; let novoNomeComp = ''; let novoPosto = '';
          if (cleanVal) {
            const userDB = usersDb.find(u => matriculasMatch(u.matricula, cleanVal));
            if (userDB) { novoNome = userDB.name; novoNomeComp = userDB.nomeCompleto; novoPosto = userDB.posto; } 
            else {
              const userSheet = (efetivoPlanilha || []).find(r => r[0] && matriculasMatch(String(r[0]).trim().toUpperCase(), cleanVal));
              if (userSheet) { novoPosto = userSheet[1] || ''; novoNomeComp = userSheet[2] || ''; novoNome = userSheet[3] || userSheet[2] || ''; }
            }
          }
          return { ...m, matricula: cleanVal, nome: novoNome, nomeCompleto: novoNomeComp, posto: novoPosto };
        }
        return m;
      });
      return { ...prev, equipe: newEquipe };
    });
  };

  const addPatrulheiro = () => {
    const num = formData.equipe.length + 1;
    setFormData(prev => ({
      ...prev,
      equipe: [...prev.equipe, { id: Date.now(), funcao: `PATRULHEIRO 0${num}`, matricula: '', nome: '', nomeCompleto: '', posto: '' }]
    }));
  };

  const removePatrulheiro = (id) => {
    setFormData(prev => ({ ...prev, equipe: prev.equipe.filter(m => m.id !== id) }));
  };

  const handleVtrSelect = (e) => {
    const v = (viaturas || []).find(v => v.id === e.target.value);
    if (v) setFormData({ ...formData, vtrId: v.id, prefixo: v.prefixo });
  };

  const handleGenericFileUpload = (e, field, isArray = false) => {
    const file = e.target.files[0];
    if (!file) return;

    if (file.type === 'application/pdf' && file.size > 400 * 1024) {
      return showToast("O arquivo PDF deve ter no máximo 400KB. Tire uma fotografia ao documento se o tamanho for superior.", "error");
    }

    const reader = new FileReader();
    reader.onload = (event) => {
      if (file.type.startsWith('image/')) {
         const img = new Image();
         img.onload = () => {
           const canvas = document.createElement('canvas');
           const MAX_DIM = 600; 
           let { width, height } = img;
           if (width > height) { if (width > MAX_DIM) { height *= MAX_DIM / width; width = MAX_DIM; } }
           else { if (height > MAX_DIM) { width *= MAX_DIM / height; height = MAX_DIM; } }
           canvas.width = width; canvas.height = height;
           const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
           ctx.drawImage(img, 0, 0, width, height);
           const compressedUrl = canvas.toDataURL('image/jpeg', 0.4); 
           
           const fileData = { url: compressedUrl, type: file.type, name: file.name };
           if (isArray) {
             setFormData(prev => ({ ...prev, [field]: [...prev[field], fileData] }));
           } else {
             setFormData(prev => ({ ...prev, [field]: fileData }));
           }
         };
         img.src = event.target.result;
      } else {
         const fileData = { url: event.target.result, type: file.type, name: file.name };
         if (isArray) {
           setFormData(prev => ({ ...prev, [field]: [...prev[field], fileData] }));
         } else {
           setFormData(prev => ({ ...prev, [field]: fileData }));
         }
      }
    };
    reader.readAsDataURL(file);
  };

  const removeGenericFile = (field, indexToRemove = null) => {
    if (indexToRemove !== null) {
       setFormData(prev => ({ ...prev, [field]: prev[field].filter((_, idx) => idx !== indexToRemove) }));
    } else {
       setFormData(prev => ({ ...prev, [field]: null }));
    }
  };

  const toggleBairroSelecionado = (bairro) => {
    setFormData(prev => ({
      ...prev,
      bairrosSelecionados: prev.bairrosSelecionados.includes(bairro)
        ? prev.bairrosSelecionados.filter(item => item !== bairro)
        : [...prev.bairrosSelecionados, bairro]
    }));
  };

  const validateStep1AndGo = () => {
const finalArea = buildAreaAtuacao(formData.opm, formData.areaSelecionada, formData.bairrosSelecionados, formData.areaDigitada);

if (!formData.dataOcorrencia || !formData.horaInicial || !formData.horaFinal) return alert("Preencha Data e Horários.");
if (!occurrenceDuration.valid) return alert(occurrenceDuration.message || "Duração da ocorrência inválida.");
if (!formData.local || !formData.natureza) return alert("Preencha o Local e selecione a Natureza da Ocorrência (Principal).");
if (formData.coordenadas && !parseCoordinates(formData.coordenadas)) return alert("Coordenadas inválidas. Use o formato: -3.6881, -40.3496");
const areaSelecionadaObj = getAreaOptionByLabel(formData.opm, formData.areaSelecionada);
if (areaSelecionadaObj && areaSelecionadaObj.bairros.length > 0 && formData.bairrosSelecionados.length === 0) {
  return alert("Selecione pelo menos um bairro da área de atuação.");
}
if (!finalArea) return alert("Preencha a Área de Atuação.");

const memInvalidos = formData.equipe.filter(m => m.matricula && !m.nome && m.matricula !== 'DEV');
if (memInvalidos.length > 0) {
    return alert(`Matrícula(s) não encontrada(s) na base de dados: ${memInvalidos.map(m => m.matricula).join(', ')}. Insira matrículas válidas ou deixe o campo em branco.`);
}

setFormData({...formData, areaAtuacao: finalArea.toUpperCase()});
setStep(2);
  };

  const submitForm = () => {
if (!formData.narrativa) return alert("A Narrativa da Ocorrência é obrigatória.");

const coordenadasGeograficas = parseCoordinates(formData.coordenadas);

onSave({
  ...formData,
  coordenadasGeograficas: coordenadasGeograficas || null,
  duracaoOcorrenciaMinutos: occurrenceDuration.totalMinutes,
  duracaoOcorrenciaHoras: occurrenceDuration.totalHours,
  duracaoOcorrenciaLabel: occurrenceDuration.label,
  dataHoraFinalCalculada: occurrenceDuration.end?.toISOString?.() || null,
  opm: formData.opm === 'OUTRA' ? formData.opmOutra : formData.opm,
  municipio: formData.municipio === 'OUTRA' ? formData.municipioOutro : formData.municipio,
  procedimento: formData.procedimento === 'OUTROS' ? formData.procedimentoOutro : formData.procedimento,
  situacaoConduzido: formData.situacaoConduzido === 'OUTRO' ? formData.situacaoConduzidoOutro.toUpperCase() : formData.situacaoConduzido,
  userId: userData?.matricula,
  userName: userData?.name,
});
  };

  const motosLivres = (viaturas || []).filter(v => v.condicao !== 'Inoperante' && v.tipoVeiculo === 'MOTO');
  const carrosLivres = (viaturas || []).filter(v => v.condicao !== 'Inoperante' && v.tipoVeiculo !== 'MOTO');
  const occurrenceFleetType = formData.tipoPoliciamento === 'MOTOPATRULHAMENTO' ? 'MOTO' : 'CARRO';
  const occurrenceFleetOptions = occurrenceFleetType === 'MOTO' ? motosLivres : carrosLivres;
  const selectedAreaObj = getAreaOptionByLabel(formData.opm, formData.areaSelecionada);
  const occurrenceDuration = useMemo(() => calculateOccurrenceDuration({
    dataOcorrencia: formData.dataOcorrencia,
    horaInicial: formData.horaInicial,
    horaFinal: formData.horaFinal
  }), [formData.dataOcorrencia, formData.horaInicial, formData.horaFinal]);

  useEffect(() => {
    setFormData(prev => {
      const equipeAtual = Array.isArray(prev.equipe) ? prev.equipe : [];
      const equipeBase = getOccurrenceDefaultTeam(prev.tipoPoliciamento, userData);
      const comandanteAtual = equipeAtual[0] || equipeBase[0];
      const isPeOuFixo = prev.tipoPoliciamento === 'POSTO FIXO' || prev.tipoPoliciamento === 'A PÉ';
      const demais = equipeAtual.slice(1).filter((m, idx) => !isPeOuFixo || m.funcao !== 'MOTORISTA');
      const equipeNormalizada = equipeBase.map((baseMembro, idx) => {
        if (idx === 0) return { ...baseMembro, ...comandanteAtual, funcao: 'COMANDANTE' };
        const candidato = demais[idx - 1] || baseMembro;
        return { ...baseMembro, ...candidato, funcao: baseMembro.funcao };
      });
      return {
        ...prev,
        equipe: equipeNormalizada,
        ...(isPeOuFixo ? { vtrId: '', prefixo: '', ht: '' } : {})
      };
    });
  }, [formData.tipoPoliciamento, userData]);


  return (
    <div className="max-w-4xl mx-auto space-y-6 pb-20">
      <div className="bg-indigo-900 text-white p-6 rounded-t-xl flex justify-between items-center shadow-lg">
        <div>
          <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold">PMCE - Relatório de Ocorrência Policial</h2>
          <p className="text-indigo-200 text-sm">Registo oficial de Produtividade Operacional.</p>
        </div>
        <ClipboardList size={40} className="text-[#ffb703] opacity-80" />
      </div>

      <div className="bg-white p-6 shadow-md rounded-b-xl border border-gray-200">
        <div className="flex border-b mb-6 pb-4 overflow-x-auto text-sm">
          {['1. Dados Básicos', '2. Fatos e Desfechos'].map((s, i) => {
             const realIndex = i + 1;
             return (
              <button key={i} onClick={() => setStep(realIndex)} disabled={step < realIndex} className={`px-4 py-2 font-bold whitespace-nowrap ${step === realIndex ? 'text-indigo-900 border-b-4 border-[#ffb703]' : 'text-gray-400'}`}>
                {s}
              </button>
             );
          })}
        </div>

        {/* STEP 1: DADOS BÁSICOS */}
        {step === 1 && (
          <div className="space-y-6 animate-fadeIn">
            
            <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-6 gap-4 bg-gray-50 p-4 rounded-lg border border-gray-200">
              <div>
                <label className="block text-xs font-bold text-gray-500 uppercase mb-1">01. Data</label>
                <input type="date" required className="w-full p-2 border rounded font-bold text-indigo-900" value={formData.dataOcorrencia} onChange={e=>setFormData({...formData, dataOcorrencia: e.target.value})} />
              </div>
              <div>
                <label className="block text-xs font-bold text-gray-500 uppercase mb-1">02. Hora Inicial</label>
                <input type="time" required className="w-full p-2 border rounded font-bold text-indigo-900" value={formData.horaInicial} onChange={e=>setFormData({...formData, horaInicial: e.target.value})} />
              </div>
              <div>
                <label className="block text-xs font-bold text-gray-500 uppercase mb-1">03. Hora Final</label>
                <input type="time" required className="w-full p-2 border rounded font-bold text-indigo-900" value={formData.horaFinal} onChange={e=>setFormData({...formData, horaFinal: e.target.value})} />
              </div>
              <div>
                <label className="block text-xs font-bold text-gray-500 uppercase mb-1">04. Turno</label>
                <select className="w-full p-2 border rounded font-bold" value={formData.turno} onChange={e=>setFormData({...formData, turno: e.target.value})}>
                  <option value="">Selecione</option>{TURNOS.map(t => <option key={t} value={t}>{t}</option>)}
                </select>
              </div>
              <div>
                <label className="block text-xs font-bold text-gray-500 uppercase mb-1">Supervisor</label>
                <input type="text" placeholder="Ex: CAP SILVA..." className="w-full p-2 border rounded font-bold text-indigo-900 uppercase" value={formData.supervisor} onChange={e=>setFormData({...formData, supervisor: e.target.value.toUpperCase()})} />
              </div>
              <div>
                <label className="block text-xs font-bold text-gray-500 uppercase mb-1">MIKE DA OCORRÊNCIA</label>
                <input type="text" placeholder="Ex: M202612345" className="w-full p-2 border rounded font-bold text-indigo-900 uppercase" value={formData.mikeOcorrencia} onChange={e=>setFormData({...formData, mikeOcorrencia: e.target.value.toUpperCase()})} />
              </div>
            </div>

            <div className={`rounded-lg border p-3 ${occurrenceDuration.valid ? 'border-emerald-200 bg-emerald-50' : 'border-amber-200 bg-amber-50'}`}>
              <p className="text-[11px] font-bold uppercase text-gray-600">Duração calculada da ocorrência</p>
              <p className={`text-base font-black mt-1 ${occurrenceDuration.valid ? 'text-emerald-700' : 'text-amber-700'}`}>{occurrenceDuration.valid ? occurrenceDuration.label : 'Informe horários válidos'}</p>
              <p className="text-[11px] text-gray-600 mt-1">{occurrenceDuration.valid ? `Encerramento calculado: ${occurrenceDuration.endDateLabel}` : 'Se a hora final for menor que a inicial, o sistema considera encerramento no dia seguinte.'}</p>
            </div>

            <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 gap-4">
              <div>
                <label className="block text-xs font-bold text-gray-500 uppercase mb-1">05. Local (Endereço Completo)</label>
                <input type="text" required placeholder="Rua, Número, Bairro..." className="w-full p-2 border rounded uppercase" value={formData.local} onChange={e=>setFormData({...formData, local: e.target.value.toUpperCase()})} />
              </div>
              <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-2">
                <div>
                  <label className="block text-xs font-bold text-gray-500 uppercase mb-1">06. Coordenadas</label>
                  <input type="text" placeholder="-3.6881, -40.3496" className="w-full p-2 border rounded" value={formData.coordenadas} onChange={e=>setFormData({...formData, coordenadas: e.target.value})} />
                  <p className="text-[10px] text-gray-500 mt-1 font-semibold">Ao informar latitude e longitude, a ocorrência será plotada automaticamente no mapa da Gestão de Produtividade.</p>
                </div>
                <div>
                  <label className="block text-xs font-bold text-gray-500 uppercase mb-1">07. Município</label>
                  <select className="w-full p-2 border rounded uppercase" value={formData.municipio} onChange={e=>setFormData({...formData, municipio: e.target.value})}>
                    <option value="">Selecione</option>{CIDADES_SERVICO.map(c => <option key={c} value={c}>{c}</option>)}
                  </select>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>

            {formData.municipio === 'OUTRA' && (
              <div>
                <label className="block text-xs font-bold text-gray-500 uppercase mb-1">Qual Município?</label>
                <input type="text" required className="w-full p-2 border rounded uppercase border-indigo-300" value={formData.municipioOutro} onChange={e=>setFormData({...formData, municipioOutro: e.target.value.toUpperCase()})} />
              </div>
            )}

            <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-3 gap-4 bg-indigo-50 p-4 rounded-lg border border-indigo-100">
              <div>
                <label className="block text-xs font-bold text-indigo-800 uppercase mb-1">08. Tipo Policiamento</label>
                <select className="w-full p-2 border border-indigo-200 rounded bg-white" value={formData.tipoPoliciamento} onChange={e=>setFormData({...formData, tipoPoliciamento: e.target.value, vtrId: '', prefixo: ''})}>
                  <option value="">Selecione</option>{MODALIDADES.map(m => <option key={m} value={m}>{m}</option>)}
                </select>
              </div>
              <div className="md:col-span-2">
                <label className="block text-xs font-bold text-indigo-800 uppercase mb-3">09. {formData.tipoPoliciamento === 'MOTOPATRULHAMENTO' ? 'Moto Principal' : 'VTR Principal'}</label>
                <FleetCardSelector
                  vehicles={occurrenceFleetOptions}
                  value={formData.vtrId}
                  onChange={(vehicleId) => {
                    const v = (viaturas || []).find(item => item.id === vehicleId);
                    if (v) setFormData(prev => ({ ...prev, vtrId: v.id, prefixo: v.prefixo }));
                    else setFormData(prev => ({ ...prev, vtrId: '', prefixo: '' }));
                  }}
                  label={formData.tipoPoliciamento === 'MOTOPATRULHAMENTO' ? 'Selecione a moto da ocorrência' : 'Selecione a viatura da ocorrência'}
                  typeFilter={occurrenceFleetType}
                />
              </div>
              <div>
                <label className="block text-xs font-bold text-indigo-800 uppercase mb-1">10. HT(s)</label>
                <input type="text" inputMode="numeric" pattern="[0-9]*" placeholder="Somente números..." className="w-full p-2 border border-indigo-200 rounded bg-white" value={formData.ht} onChange={e=>setFormData({...formData, ht: sanitizeNumericInput(e.target.value)})} />
              </div>
            </div>

            <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 gap-4 bg-indigo-50 p-4 rounded-lg border border-indigo-100">
              <div>
                <label className="block text-xs font-bold text-indigo-800 uppercase mb-1">OPM da Ocorrência</label>
                <select className="w-full p-2 border border-indigo-200 rounded bg-white" value={formData.opm} onChange={e=>setFormData({...formData, opm: e.target.value, areaSelecionada: '', bairrosSelecionados: [], areaDigitada: ''})}>
                  <option value="">Selecione</option>{OPMS.map(o => <option key={o} value={o}>{o}</option>)}
                </select>
                {formData.opm === 'OUTRA' && (
                  <input type="text" placeholder="Qual OPM?" className="w-full p-2 border border-indigo-200 rounded bg-white uppercase mt-2" value={formData.opmOutra} onChange={e=>setFormData({...formData, opmOutra: e.target.value.toUpperCase()})} />
                )}
              </div>
              <div>
                <label className="block text-xs font-bold text-indigo-800 uppercase mb-1 flex items-center"><MapPin size={14} className="mr-1"/> Área de Atuação</label>
                {AREAS_POR_OPM[formData.opm] ? (
                  <div className="space-y-3">
                    <select 
                      className="w-full p-2 border border-indigo-200 rounded bg-white uppercase" 
                      value={formData.areaSelecionada} 
                      onChange={e => setFormData({...formData, areaSelecionada: e.target.value, bairrosSelecionados: [], areaDigitada: ''})}
                    >
                      <option value="">Selecione</option>
                      {getAreaOptionsByOpm(formData.opm).map(area => <option key={area.label} value={area.label}>{area.label}</option>)}
                    </select>

                    {formData.areaSelecionada && formData.areaSelecionada !== 'OUTRA' && selectedAreaObj && selectedAreaObj.bairros.length > 0 && (
                      <div className="border border-indigo-200 rounded-lg bg-white p-3">
                        <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-2 gap-2">
                          <span className="text-[11px] font-bold text-indigo-700 uppercase">Bairros da {formData.areaSelecionada}</span>
                          <div className="flex gap-2">
                            <button type="button" onClick={() => setFormData(prev => ({ ...prev, bairrosSelecionados: getAreaOptionByLabel(prev.opm, prev.areaSelecionada)?.bairros || [] }))} className="text-[10px] font-bold text-blue-700 hover:underline">Marcar todos</button>
                            <button type="button" onClick={() => setFormData(prev => ({ ...prev, bairrosSelecionados: [] }))} className="text-[10px] font-bold text-red-600 hover:underline">Limpar</button>
                          </div>
                        </div>
                        <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 gap-2">
                          {(selectedAreaObj?.bairros || []).map(bairro => (
                            <label key={bairro} className="flex items-center gap-2 text-xs font-semibold text-gray-700 bg-indigo-50 border border-indigo-100 rounded px-2 py-2">
                              <input type="checkbox" checked={formData.bairrosSelecionados.includes(bairro)} onChange={() => toggleBairroSelecionado(bairro)} className="accent-indigo-700" />
                              <span>{bairro}</span>
                            </label>
                          ))}
                        </div>
                      </div>
                    )}

                    {formData.areaSelecionada && formData.areaSelecionada !== 'OUTRA' && selectedAreaObj && selectedAreaObj.bairros.length === 0 && (
                      <div className="border border-indigo-200 rounded-lg bg-indigo-50 p-3 text-xs font-semibold text-indigo-800">
                        Área selecionada sem subdivisão de bairros. Basta manter esta opção selecionada.
                      </div>
                    )}

                  </div>
                ) : (
                  <input type="text" placeholder="Relacione os bairros ou área..." className="w-full p-2 border border-indigo-200 rounded bg-white uppercase" value={formData.areaDigitada} onChange={e=>setFormData({...formData, areaDigitada: e.target.value.toUpperCase()})} disabled={formData.opm !== 'OUTRA'} />
                )}
                {formData.opm !== 'OUTRA' && !AREAS_POR_OPM[formData.opm] && (
                  <p className="mt-2 text-[11px] font-semibold text-amber-700 bg-amber-50 border border-amber-200 rounded px-2 py-2">A digitação manual da área só é liberada quando a OPM selecionada for OUTRA.</p>
                )}
              </div>
            </div>

            <div>
               <label className="block text-sm font-bold text-gray-700 mb-2 border-b pb-1">Composição da Equipe (11 a 14)</label>
               {formData.equipe.map((membro, index) => (
                  <div key={membro.id} className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-3 gap-4 mb-3 items-end">
                    <div className="md:col-span-1">
                      <label className="block text-xs font-bold text-gray-500 uppercase mb-1">{membro.funcao}</label>
                      <input type="text" placeholder="Matrícula" className="w-full p-2 border rounded font-mono uppercase" value={membro.matricula} onChange={e => handleMatriculaChange(membro.id, e.target.value)} />
                    </div>
                    <div className="md:col-span-2 flex items-center space-x-2">
                      <input type="text" readOnly className="w-full p-2 border rounded bg-gray-100 text-gray-600 uppercase text-sm" value={membro.nome ? `${membro.posto} ${membro.nome}` : ''} placeholder="Nome Auto-preenchido..." />
                      {index > 3 && (
                        <button onClick={() => removePatrulheiro(membro.id)} className="text-red-500 p-2 hover:bg-red-50 rounded"><Trash2 size={18}/></button>
                      )}
                    </div>
                  </div>
               ))}
               <button onClick={addPatrulheiro} className="text-indigo-600 font-bold text-xs flex items-center hover:underline mt-2"><Plus size={14} className="mr-1"/> Adicionar mais Patrulheiros</button>
            </div>

            <div>
              <label className="block text-xs font-bold text-gray-500 uppercase mb-1">15. Composições no Apoio</label>
              <input type="text" placeholder="Ex: CP-3045, RAIO 01..." className="w-full p-2 border rounded uppercase" value={formData.apoio} onChange={e=>setFormData({...formData, apoio: e.target.value.toUpperCase()})} />
            </div>

            <div>
              <label className="block text-xs font-bold text-gray-500 uppercase mb-1">16. Natureza da Ocorrência (Principal) <span className="text-red-600">*</span></label>
              <select
                required
                className={`w-full p-3 border-2 rounded uppercase font-bold focus:ring-indigo-500 ${!formData.natureza ? 'border-red-300 bg-red-50 text-red-700' : formData.natureza.includes('(CVLI)') ? 'border-red-400 bg-red-50 text-red-900' : formData.natureza.includes('(CVP)') ? 'border-amber-400 bg-amber-50 text-amber-900' : 'border-indigo-300 bg-indigo-50 text-indigo-900'}`}
                value={formData.natureza}
                onChange={e=>setFormData({...formData, natureza: e.target.value.toUpperCase()})}
              >
                <option value="">Selecione</option>
                {NATUREZAS_OCORRENCIA.map(n => <option key={n} value={n}>{n}</option>)}
              </select>
              <div className="mt-2 flex flex-wrap gap-2 text-[11px] font-bold uppercase">
                <span className="px-2 py-1 rounded-full bg-red-100 text-red-700 border border-red-200">CVLI / maior gravidade</span>
                <span className="px-2 py-1 rounded-full bg-amber-100 text-amber-700 border border-amber-200">CVP / patrimoniais</span>
                <span className="px-2 py-1 rounded-full bg-indigo-100 text-indigo-700 border border-indigo-200">Demais naturezas</span>
              </div>
            </div>

            <div className="flex justify-end mt-6">
              <button onClick={validateStep1AndGo} className="bg-indigo-900 text-white px-6 py-2 rounded font-bold hover:bg-indigo-800 shadow flex items-center">Avançar <ArrowUp size={18} className="ml-1 rotate-90"/></button>
            </div>
          </div>
        )}

        {/* STEP 2: FATOS E DESFECHOS */}
        {step === 2 && (
          <div className="space-y-6 animate-fadeIn">
            
            <div>
              <label className="block text-xs font-bold text-gray-500 uppercase mb-1">17. Narrativa da Ocorrência</label>
              <textarea required rows="6" placeholder="Relate os fatos de forma clara e objetiva..." className="w-full p-3 border rounded uppercase bg-gray-50 focus:bg-white focus:ring-2 focus:ring-indigo-500" value={formData.narrativa} onChange={e=>setFormData({...formData, narrativa: e.target.value.toUpperCase()})}></textarea>
            </div>

            <div className="bg-orange-50 p-4 rounded-lg border border-orange-200 space-y-4">
              <h3 className="font-bold text-orange-900 border-b border-orange-200 pb-1 flex items-center"><Crosshair size={18} className="mr-2"/> Apreensões e Materiais</h3>
              
              <div>
                <label className="block text-xs font-bold text-orange-800 uppercase mb-1">18. Material Apresentado (Geral)</label>
                <input type="text" className="w-full p-2 border rounded uppercase" value={formData.materialApresentado} onChange={e=>setFormData({...formData, materialApresentado: e.target.value.toUpperCase()})} />
              </div>
              <div>
                <label className="block text-xs font-bold text-orange-800 uppercase mb-1">19. Veículo(s) [Marca/Modelo/Cor/Placa]</label>
                <input type="text" className="w-full p-2 border rounded uppercase" value={formData.veiculos} onChange={e=>setFormData({...formData, veiculos: e.target.value.toUpperCase()})} />
              </div>
              <div>
                <label className="block text-xs font-bold text-orange-800 uppercase mb-1">20. Arma(s) [Tipo/Marca/Calibre/Numeração/Munições]</label>
                <input type="text" placeholder="Ex: 01 REVÓLVER TAURUS CAL 38..." className="w-full p-2 border rounded uppercase" value={formData.armas} onChange={e=>setFormData({...formData, armas: e.target.value.toUpperCase()})} />
              </div>
              <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 gap-4">
                <div>
                  <label className="block text-xs font-bold text-orange-800 uppercase mb-1">21. Entorpecente(s) [Tipo/Qtd(g)]</label>
                  <input type="text" placeholder="Ex: MACONHA 50g, COCAÍNA 10g..." className="w-full p-2 border rounded uppercase" value={formData.entorpecentes} onChange={e=>setFormData({...formData, entorpecentes: e.target.value.toUpperCase()})} />
                </div>
                <div>
                  <label className="block text-xs font-bold text-orange-800 uppercase mb-1">22. Valores Apreendidos (R$)</label>
                  <input type="text" placeholder="R$ 1.500,00" className="w-full p-2 border rounded uppercase font-bold text-green-700" value={formData.valores} onChange={e=>setFormData({...formData, valores: e.target.value.toUpperCase()})} />
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>

            <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 gap-4">
              <div>
                <label className="block text-xs font-bold text-gray-500 uppercase mb-1">23. Envolvido(s) / Vítimas</label>
                <textarea rows="3" placeholder="Nome, Idade, CPF..." className="w-full p-2 border rounded uppercase" value={formData.envolvidos} onChange={e=>setFormData({...formData, envolvidos: e.target.value.toUpperCase()})}></textarea>
              </div>
              <div>
                <label className="block text-xs font-bold text-gray-500 uppercase mb-1">24. Suspeito(s) / Conduzidos</label>
                <textarea rows="3" placeholder="Nome, Idade, CPF, Alcunha..." className="w-full p-2 border rounded uppercase" value={formData.suspeitos} onChange={e=>setFormData({...formData, suspeitos: e.target.value.toUpperCase()})}></textarea>
              </div>
            </div>

            <div className="bg-indigo-50 p-4 rounded-lg border border-indigo-200 space-y-4">
              <h3 className="font-bold text-indigo-900 border-b border-indigo-200 pb-1 flex items-center"><Gavel size={18} className="mr-2"/> Desfecho e Procedimentos</h3>
              
              <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 gap-4">
                <div>
                  <label className="block text-xs font-bold text-indigo-800 uppercase mb-1">25. Tipo do Procedimento</label>
                  <select className="w-full p-2 border border-indigo-200 rounded uppercase font-bold bg-white focus:ring-indigo-500" value={formData.procedimento} onChange={e=>setFormData({...formData, procedimento: e.target.value})}>
                    <option value="">Selecione</option>{PROCEDIMENTOS.map(p => <option key={p} value={p}>{p}</option>)}
                  </select>
                  {formData.procedimento === 'OUTROS' && (
                    <input type="text" placeholder="Qual?" className="w-full p-2 border border-indigo-200 rounded mt-2 uppercase bg-white" value={formData.procedimentoOutro} onChange={e=>setFormData({...formData, procedimentoOutro: e.target.value.toUpperCase()})} />
                  )}
                </div>
                <div>
                  <label className="block text-xs font-bold text-indigo-800 uppercase mb-1">Anexar Documento do Procedimento</label>
                  {formData.anexoProcedimento ? (
                    <div className="flex items-center justify-between p-2 bg-white border border-indigo-200 rounded text-sm">
                      <span className="truncate text-indigo-700 mr-2 font-semibold flex items-center">
                        <CheckCircle size={14} className="mr-1"/> {formData.anexoProcedimento.name}
                      </span>
                      <button onClick={() => removeGenericFile('anexoProcedimento')} className="text-red-500 hover:text-red-700 flex-shrink-0"><XCircle size={16}/></button>
                    </div>
                  ) : (
                    <label className="flex items-center justify-center w-full p-2 border border-dashed border-indigo-400 bg-white text-indigo-600 rounded cursor-pointer hover:bg-indigo-100 transition font-bold text-xs">
                      <Paperclip size={16} className="mr-1"/> Anexar Arquivo (PDF ou Imagem)
                      <input type="file" accept="image/*,application/pdf" className="hidden" onChange={(e) => handleGenericFileUpload(e, 'anexoProcedimento')} />
                    </label>
                  )}
                </div>
              </div>
              
              <div>
                <label className="block text-xs font-bold text-indigo-800 uppercase mb-1">26. Capitulação Legal (Artigos)</label>
                <input type="text" placeholder="Ex: Art. 33 da Lei 11.343/06 (Tráfico)" className="w-full p-2 border border-indigo-200 rounded uppercase bg-white" value={formData.capitulacao} onChange={e=>setFormData({...formData, capitulacao: e.target.value.toUpperCase()})} />
              </div>

              <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-3 gap-4">
                <div>
                  <label className="block text-xs font-bold text-indigo-800 uppercase mb-1">27. Situação do Conduzido</label>
                  <select className="w-full p-2 border border-indigo-200 rounded uppercase bg-white" value={formData.situacaoConduzido} onChange={e=>setFormData({...formData, situacaoConduzido: e.target.value})}>
                    <option>LIBERADO</option><option>PRESO / APREENDIDO</option><option>NÃO HOUVE CONDUZIDO</option><option>OUTRO</option>
                  </select>
                  {formData.situacaoConduzido === 'OUTRO' && (
                    <input type="text" placeholder="Descreva a Situação..." className="w-full p-2 border border-indigo-200 rounded mt-2 uppercase bg-white" value={formData.situacaoConduzidoOutro} onChange={e=>setFormData({...formData, situacaoConduzidoOutro: e.target.value.toUpperCase()})} />
                  )}
                </div>
                <div>
                  <label className="block text-xs font-bold text-indigo-800 uppercase mb-1">28. Delegado(a)</label>
                  <input type="text" className="w-full p-2 border border-indigo-200 rounded uppercase bg-white" value={formData.delegado} onChange={e=>setFormData({...formData, delegado: e.target.value.toUpperCase()})} />
                </div>
                <div>
                  <label className="block text-xs font-bold text-indigo-800 uppercase mb-1">29. Escrivão(ã)</label>
                  <input type="text" className="w-full p-2 border border-indigo-200 rounded uppercase bg-white" value={formData.escrivao} onChange={e=>setFormData({...formData, escrivao: e.target.value.toUpperCase()})} />
                </div>
              </div>

              <div>
                <label className="block text-xs font-bold text-indigo-800 uppercase mb-1">30. Comentários Adicionais</label>
                <input type="text" className="w-full p-2 border border-indigo-200 rounded uppercase bg-white" value={formData.comentarios} onChange={e=>setFormData({...formData, comentarios: e.target.value.toUpperCase()})} />
              </div>
            </div>

            <div className="bg-gray-50 p-4 rounded-lg border border-gray-200 mt-4">
              <h3 className="font-bold text-gray-800 border-b pb-1 mb-3 flex items-center"><Paperclip size={18} className="mr-2"/> Anexos Gerais da Ocorrência</h3>
              <p className="text-xs text-gray-500 mb-4">Adicione fotos do material apreendido, local do crime, ou outros documentos relevantes.</p>
              
              <div className="grid grid-cols-2 md:grid-cols-4 gap-3">
                {formData.anexosGerais.map((anexo, index) => (
                  <div key={index} className="relative h-24 rounded border border-gray-300 bg-white flex flex-col items-center justify-center overflow-hidden shadow-sm">
                    {anexo.type.includes('image') ? (
                      <img src={anexo.url} alt="Anexo" className="w-full h-full object-cover" />
                    ) : (
                      <div className="flex flex-col items-center justify-center p-2 text-indigo-700">
                        <FileText size={24} className="mb-1"/>
                        <span className="text-[9px] text-center font-bold break-words line-clamp-2 w-full">{anexo.name}</span>
                      </div>
                    )}
                    <button onClick={() => removeGenericFile('anexosGerais', index)} className="absolute top-1 right-1 bg-red-500 text-white rounded p-1 hover:bg-red-600 shadow"><Trash2 size={12}/></button>
                  </div>
                ))}
                
                <label className="flex flex-col items-center justify-center h-24 rounded border-2 border-dashed border-gray-400 bg-white text-gray-500 cursor-pointer hover:bg-gray-100 hover:text-indigo-600 transition">
                  <Plus size={24} className="mb-1"/>
                  <span className="text-[10px] font-bold">Novo Anexo</span>
                  <input type="file" accept="image/*,application/pdf" className="hidden" onChange={(e) => handleGenericFileUpload(e, 'anexosGerais', true)} />
                </label>
              </div>
            </div>

            <div className="flex justify-between mt-6 pt-4 border-t border-gray-300">
              <button onClick={() => setStep(1)} className="text-gray-600 px-6 py-2 rounded font-bold border hover:bg-gray-50">⬅ Voltar</button>
              <button onClick={submitForm} className="bg-indigo-900 text-white px-6 py-3 rounded-lg font-bold hover:bg-indigo-800 shadow-lg text-lg flex items-center">
                <CheckCircle className="mr-2"/> SALVAR OCORRÊNCIA
              </button>
            </div>
          </div>
        )}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}


function GeoOccurrencesMap({ ocorrencias = [] }) {
  const mapContainerRef = useRef(null);
  const mapInstanceRef = useRef(null);
  const layerRef = useRef(null);
  const [leafletError, setLeafletError] = useState('');

  useEffect(() => {
    let cancelled = false;

    ensureLeafletAssets()
      .then((L) => {
        if (cancelled || !mapContainerRef.current || !L) return;

        if (!mapInstanceRef.current) {
          mapInstanceRef.current = L.map(mapContainerRef.current, { zoomControl: true }).setView([-3.6881, -40.3496], 11);
          L.tileLayer('https://{s}.tile.openstreetmap.org/{z}/{x}/{y}.png', {
            maxZoom: 19,
            attribution: '&copy; OpenStreetMap'
          }).addTo(mapInstanceRef.current);
        }

        if (layerRef.current) {
          layerRef.current.clearLayers();
        } else {
          layerRef.current = L.layerGroup().addTo(mapInstanceRef.current);
        }

        const markers = [];
        ocorrencias.forEach((item) => {
          const geo = item?.coordenadasGeograficas || parseCoordinates(item?.coordenadas);
          if (!geo) return;

          const marker = L.circleMarker([geo.lat, geo.lng], {
            radius: 7,
            weight: 2,
            color: '#312e81',
            fillColor: '#ffb703',
            fillOpacity: 0.85
          });

          const popup = `
            <div style="min-width:220px">
              <strong>${item.natureza || 'Ocorrência'}</strong><br/>
              <span><b>Data:</b> ${item.dataOcorrencia ? item.dataOcorrencia.split('-').reverse().join('/') : '-'} ${item.horaInicial || ''}</span><br/>
              <span><b>Local:</b> ${item.local || 'N/I'}</span><br/>
              <span><b>Município:</b> ${item.municipio || 'N/I'}</span><br/>
              <span><b>Duração:</b> ${item.duracaoOcorrenciaLabel || 'N/I'}</span><br/><span><b>Coord.:</b> ${geo.lat.toFixed(5)}, ${geo.lng.toFixed(5)}</span>
            </div>
          `;

          marker.bindPopup(popup);
          marker.addTo(layerRef.current);
          markers.push(marker);
        });

        if (markers.length > 0) {
          const group = L.featureGroup(markers);
          mapInstanceRef.current.fitBounds(group.getBounds().pad(0.25));
        } else {
          mapInstanceRef.current.setView([-3.6881, -40.3496], 11);
        }

        setTimeout(() => mapInstanceRef.current?.invalidateSize(), 150);
      })
      .catch((error) => {
        if (!cancelled) setLeafletError(error.message || 'Falha ao carregar o mapa.');
      });

    return () => {
      cancelled = true;
    };
  }, [ocorrencias]);

  useEffect(() => {
    return () => {
      if (mapInstanceRef.current) {
        mapInstanceRef.current.remove();
        mapInstanceRef.current = null;
      }
    };
  }, []);

  if (leafletError) {
    return <div className="rounded-xl border border-red-200 bg-red-50 p-4 text-sm font-bold text-red-700">{leafletError}</div>;
  }

  return <div ref={mapContainerRef} className="w-full h-[420px] rounded-xl border border-indigo-200 overflow-hidden" />;
}

function GeoOccurrenceAnalytics({ ocorrencias = [] }) {
  const ocorrenciasGeorreferenciadas = useMemo(() => {
    return (ocorrencias || [])
      .map(item => {
        const geo = item?.coordenadasGeograficas || parseCoordinates(item?.coordenadas);
        return geo ? { ...item, geo } : null;
      })
      .filter(Boolean);
  }, [ocorrencias]);

  const hotspots = useMemo(() => {
    const grouped = ocorrenciasGeorreferenciadas.reduce((acc, item) => {
      const key = buildGeoHotspotKey(item.geo);
      if (!key) return acc;
      if (!acc[key]) {
        acc[key] = {
          key,
          lat: Number(item.geo.lat.toFixed(3)),
          lng: Number(item.geo.lng.toFixed(3)),
          total: 0,
          naturezas: {},
          municipios: {},
          exemplos: []
        };
      }
      acc[key].total += 1;
      acc[key].naturezas[item.natureza || 'SEM NATUREZA'] = (acc[key].naturezas[item.natureza || 'SEM NATUREZA'] || 0) + 1;
      acc[key].municipios[item.municipio || 'N/I'] = (acc[key].municipios[item.municipio || 'N/I'] || 0) + 1;
      if (acc[key].exemplos.length < 3) acc[key].exemplos.push(item.local || 'Local não informado');
      return acc;
    }, {});

    return Object.values(grouped)
      .map(item => ({
        ...item,
        naturezaPredominante: Object.entries(item.naturezas).sort((a, b) => b[1] - a[1])[0]?.[0] || 'N/I',
        municipioPredominante: Object.entries(item.municipios).sort((a, b) => b[1] - a[1])[0]?.[0] || 'N/I'
      }))
      .sort((a, b) => b.total - a.total)
      .slice(0, 8);
  }, [ocorrenciasGeorreferenciadas]);

  const naturezasGeograficas = useMemo(() => {
    return Object.entries(
      ocorrenciasGeorreferenciadas.reduce((acc, item) => {
        const key = item.natureza || 'SEM NATUREZA';
        acc[key] = (acc[key] || 0) + 1;
        return acc;
      }, {})
    )
      .sort((a, b) => b[1] - a[1])
      .slice(0, 6);
  }, [ocorrenciasGeorreferenciadas]);

  return (
    <div className="space-y-4">
      <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-3 gap-4">
        <div className="bg-white p-4 rounded-xl border border-indigo-200 shadow-sm">
          <p className="text-[11px] font-bold uppercase text-indigo-700">Ocorrências mapeadas</p>
          <div className="text-3xl font-black text-indigo-900 mt-1">{ocorrenciasGeorreferenciadas.length}</div>
          <p className="text-xs text-gray-500 mt-1">Registros com latitude e longitude válidas.</p>
        </div>
        <div className="bg-white p-4 rounded-xl border border-indigo-200 shadow-sm">
          <p className="text-[11px] font-bold uppercase text-indigo-700">Pontos quentes</p>
          <div className="text-3xl font-black text-indigo-900 mt-1">{hotspots.length}</div>
          <p className="text-xs text-gray-500 mt-1">Agrupamento aproximado por área geográfica.</p>
        </div>
        <div className="bg-white p-4 rounded-xl border border-indigo-200 shadow-sm">
          <p className="text-[11px] font-bold uppercase text-indigo-700">Natureza líder no mapa</p>
          <div className="text-base font-black text-indigo-900 mt-2">{naturezasGeograficas[0]?.[0] || 'Sem dados'}</div>
          <p className="text-xs text-gray-500 mt-1">{naturezasGeograficas[0]?.[1] || 0} ocorrência(s) georreferenciada(s).</p>
        </div>
      </div>

      <div className="grid grid-cols-1 lg:grid-cols-2 gap-4">
        <div className="bg-white p-4 rounded-xl border border-indigo-200 shadow-sm">
          <h3 className="text-sm font-bold text-indigo-900 uppercase mb-3">Top áreas mapeadas</h3>
          <div className="space-y-3">
            {hotspots.length === 0 && <p className="text-sm text-gray-500">Nenhuma ocorrência com coordenadas válidas para consolidar.</p>}
            {hotspots.map((item, index) => (
              <div key={item.key} className="rounded-lg border border-gray-200 p-3 bg-gray-50">
                <div className="flex items-center justify-between gap-3">
                  <div>
                    <p className="text-xs font-bold uppercase text-indigo-700">#{index + 1} • {item.municipioPredominante}</p>
                    <h4 className="font-bold text-gray-800">{item.naturezaPredominante}</h4>
                    <p className="text-xs text-gray-500">Centro aproximado: {item.lat.toFixed(3)}, {item.lng.toFixed(3)}</p>
                  </div>
                  <span className="text-2xl font-black text-indigo-900">{item.total}</span>
                </div>
                {item.exemplos.length > 0 && <p className="text-xs text-gray-600 mt-2">Ex.: {item.exemplos.join(' | ')}</p>}
              </div>
            ))}
          </div>
        </div>

        <div className="bg-white p-4 rounded-xl border border-indigo-200 shadow-sm">
          <h3 className="text-sm font-bold text-indigo-900 uppercase mb-3">Naturezas mais recorrentes no mapa</h3>
          <div className="space-y-3">
            {naturezasGeograficas.length === 0 && <p className="text-sm text-gray-500">Sem ocorrências georreferenciadas para análise estatística.</p>}
            {naturezasGeograficas.map(([natureza, total]) => (
              <div key={natureza} className="flex items-center justify-between rounded-lg border border-gray-200 bg-gray-50 px-3 py-3">
                <span className="text-sm font-bold text-gray-800 pr-3">{natureza}</span>
                <span className="text-xl font-black text-indigo-900">{total}</span>
              </div>
            ))}
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>

      <GeoOccurrencesMap ocorrencias={ocorrenciasGeorreferenciadas} />
    </div>
  );
}

function OcorrenciaHistory({ ocorrencias, setPrintLayout, setViewOcorrencia, isGestor, isDev, onDelete }) {
  const [filterDataIni, setFilterDataIni] = useState('');
  const [filterDataFim, setFilterDataFim] = useState('');
  const [filterNatureza, setFilterNatureza] = useState('');
  const [filterPolicial, setFilterPolicial] = useState('');
  const [kpiFilter, setKpiFilter] = useState('all');
  const [showGeoMap, setShowGeoMap] = useState(true);

  const baseFilteredOcs = (ocorrencias || []).filter(c => {
    if (filterDataIni && c.dataOcorrencia < filterDataIni) return false;
    if (filterDataFim && c.dataOcorrencia > filterDataFim) return false;
    if (filterNatureza && !(c.natureza || '').includes(filterNatureza)) return false;
    if (filterPolicial) {
       const hasPM = c.equipe?.some(eq => eq.matricula.includes(filterPolicial) || (eq.nome||'').toUpperCase().includes(filterPolicial));
       if (!hasPM) return false;
    }
    return true;
  });

  const totalCVLI = baseFilteredOcs.filter(c => (c.natureza || '').includes('CVLI')).length;
  const totalCVP = baseFilteredOcs.filter(c => (c.natureza || '').includes('CVP')).length;

  const totalArmas = baseFilteredOcs.filter(c => c.armas && c.armas.length > 3).length;
  const totalDrogas = baseFilteredOcs.filter(c => c.entorpecentes && c.entorpecentes.length > 3).length;
  const totalProcedimentos = baseFilteredOcs.filter(c => c.procedimento !== 'OUTROS' && c.procedimento !== '').length;
  const totalPrisoes = baseFilteredOcs.filter(c => c.situacaoConduzido === 'PRESO / APREENDIDO').length;

  const filteredOcs = baseFilteredOcs.filter(c => {
    if (kpiFilter === 'cvli' && !(c.natureza || '').includes('CVLI')) return false;
    if (kpiFilter === 'cvp' && !(c.natureza || '').includes('CVP')) return false;
    if (kpiFilter === 'armas' && !(c.armas && c.armas.length > 3)) return false;
    if (kpiFilter === 'drogas' && !(c.entorpecentes && c.entorpecentes.length > 3)) return false;
    if (kpiFilter === 'prisoes' && c.situacaoConduzido !== 'PRESO / APREENDIDO') return false;
    if (kpiFilter === 'procedimentos' && (c.procedimento === 'OUTROS' || c.procedimento === '')) return false;
    return true;
  });

  const ocorrenciasGeorreferenciadas = useMemo(() => {
    return filteredOcs.filter(item => item?.coordenadasGeograficas || parseCoordinates(item?.coordenadas));
  }, [filteredOcs]);
  const duracaoPorNatureza = useMemo(() => {
    return Object.entries(
      filteredOcs.reduce((acc, item) => {
        const natureza = item.natureza || 'SEM NATUREZA';
        const minutos = Number(item.duracaoOcorrenciaMinutos);
        if (!Number.isFinite(minutos) || minutos <= 0) return acc;
        if (!acc[natureza]) acc[natureza] = { totalMinutos: 0, totalOcorrencias: 0 };
        acc[natureza].totalMinutos += minutos;
        acc[natureza].totalOcorrencias += 1;
        return acc;
      }, {})
    ).map(([natureza, dados]) => ({
      natureza,
      totalOcorrencias: dados.totalOcorrencias,
      mediaMinutos: Math.round(dados.totalMinutos / dados.totalOcorrencias),
      mediaLabel: `${Math.floor((dados.totalMinutos / dados.totalOcorrencias) / 60)}h${String(Math.round((dados.totalMinutos / dados.totalOcorrencias) % 60)).padStart(2, '0')}min`
    })).sort((a, b) => b.mediaMinutos - a.mediaMinutos).slice(0, 8);
  }, [filteredOcs]);

  const ocorrenciaMaisRapida = useMemo(() => duracaoPorNatureza.slice().sort((a, b) => a.mediaMinutos - b.mediaMinutos)[0] || null, [duracaoPorNatureza]);
  const ocorrenciaMaisLenta = useMemo(() => duracaoPorNatureza[0] || null, [duracaoPorNatureza]);

  const exportCSV = () => {
    const headers = [
      'ID', '01-Data', '02-HoraIni', '03-HoraFim', '03A-DuracaoMin', '03B-DuracaoLabel', '04-Turno', 'Supervisor', 'MIKE DA OCORRÊNCIA', 'OPM', 'Area Atuacao', '05-Local', '06-Coordenadas', 'Latitude', 'Longitude', '07-Municipio', 
      '08-Policiamento', '09-VTR', '10-HT', 'Equipe Completa (Posto-Nome-Mat)', '15-Apoio', '16-Natureza', '17-Narrativa', 
      '18-Material', '19-Veiculos', '20-Armas', '21-Drogas', '22-Valores', '23-Envolvidos', '24-Suspeitos',
      '25-Procedimento', '26-Capitulacao', '27-SitConduzido', '28-Delegado', '29-Escrivao', '30-Comentarios'
    ];
    
    const rows = filteredOcs.map(c => {
      const equipeStr = c.equipe?.map(e => `${e.funcao}: ${e.posto} ${e.nome} (${e.matricula})`).join(' | ');
      
      const geo = c.coordenadasGeograficas || parseCoordinates(c.coordenadas);
      const fields = [
        c.id, c.dataOcorrencia, c.horaInicial, c.horaFinal, c.duracaoOcorrenciaMinutos ?? '', c.duracaoOcorrenciaLabel ?? '', c.turno, c.supervisor, c.mikeOcorrencia, c.opm, c.areaAtuacao, c.local, c.coordenadas, geo?.lat ?? '', geo?.lng ?? '', c.municipio,
        c.tipoPoliciamento, c.prefixo, c.ht, equipeStr, c.apoio, c.natureza, c.narrativa,
        c.materialApresentado, c.veiculos, c.armas, c.entorpecentes, c.valores, c.envolvidos, c.suspeitos,
        c.procedimento, c.capitulacao, c.situacaoConduzido, c.delegado, c.escrivao, c.comentarios
      ];
      
      return fields.map(f => `"${String(f ?? '').replace(/"/g, '""')}"`).join(';');
    });
    
    const csvContent = "\uFEFF" + [headers.join(';'), ...rows].join('\n');
    const blob = new Blob([csvContent], { type: 'text/csv;charset=utf-8;' });
    const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
    const link = document.createElement('a');
    link.href = url;
    link.setAttribute('download', 'Produtividade_Ocorrencias.csv');
    document.body.appendChild(link);
    link.click();
    document.body.removeChild(link);
  };

  const handlePrintResumo = () => {
    setPrintLayout({
      type: 'resumo_ocorrencias',
      data: filteredOcs,
      filters: { 
        dataIni: filterDataIni, 
        dataFim: filterDataFim
      }
    });
  };

  return (
    <div className="space-y-6">
      <div className="flex flex-col md:flex-row md:justify-between md:items-end space-y-4 md:space-y-0">
        <div>
          <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold text-indigo-900">{isGestor ? 'Gestão de Produtividade' : 'Minha Produtividade'}</h2>
          <p className="text-gray-500 text-sm">Histórico de Ocorrências Policiais Registradas.</p>
        </div>
        <div className="flex items-end space-x-2">
          <button onClick={handlePrintResumo} className="bg-gray-800 text-white px-3 py-2 rounded-lg flex items-center shadow-sm text-xs font-bold h-[38px] hover:bg-gray-700">
            <Printer size={16} className="mr-1" /> Imprimir Resumo
          </button>
          <button onClick={exportCSV} className="bg-indigo-900 text-white px-3 py-2 rounded-lg flex items-center shadow-sm text-xs font-bold h-[38px] hover:bg-indigo-800">
            <Download size={16} className="mr-1" /> Exportar Dados
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>

      {isGestor && (
        <div className="space-y-4 mb-6">
          {/* MACRO KPIs */}
          <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 gap-4">
            <button onClick={() => setKpiFilter('cvli')} className={`bg-white p-5 rounded-xl shadow-sm border-l-4 flex justify-between items-center transition hover:scale-105 ${kpiFilter === 'cvli' ? 'border-red-700 ring-2 ring-red-200' : 'border-red-400'}`}>
              <div className="text-left">
                <p className="text-gray-500 text-[11px] font-bold uppercase mb-1">Indicador Macro</p>
                <h3 className="font-bold text-red-700 text-lg">CVLI <span className="text-xs font-normal text-gray-600 block">Crimes Violentos Letais Intencionais</span></h3>
              </div>
              <span className="text-4xl font-black text-red-700">{totalCVLI}</span>
            </button>
            <button onClick={() => setKpiFilter('cvp')} className={`bg-white p-5 rounded-xl shadow-sm border-l-4 flex justify-between items-center transition hover:scale-105 ${kpiFilter === 'cvp' ? 'border-orange-600 ring-2 ring-orange-200' : 'border-orange-300'}`}>
              <div className="text-left">
                <p className="text-gray-500 text-[11px] font-bold uppercase mb-1">Indicador Macro</p>
                <h3 className="font-bold text-orange-600 text-lg">CVP <span className="text-xs font-normal text-gray-600 block">Crimes Contra o Patrimônio</span></h3>
              </div>
              <span className="text-4xl font-black text-orange-600">{totalCVP}</span>
            </button>
          </div>

          {/* MICRO KPIs */}
          <div className="grid grid-cols-2 md:grid-cols-5 gap-4">
            <button onClick={() => setKpiFilter('all')} className={`bg-white p-4 rounded-xl shadow-sm border-l-4 flex flex-col justify-center text-left transition hover:scale-105 ${kpiFilter === 'all' ? 'border-indigo-600 ring-2 ring-indigo-200' : 'border-indigo-300'}`}>
              <p className="text-gray-500 text-[10px] font-bold uppercase mb-1">Total Ocorrências</p>
              <div className="flex items-center"><ClipboardList className="text-indigo-600 mr-2" size={20}/><span className="text-2xl font-bold">{baseFilteredOcs.length}</span></div>
            </button>
            <button onClick={() => setKpiFilter('armas')} className={`bg-white p-4 rounded-xl shadow-sm border-l-4 flex flex-col justify-center text-left transition hover:scale-105 ${kpiFilter === 'armas' ? 'border-orange-500 ring-2 ring-orange-200' : 'border-orange-300'}`}>
              <p className="text-gray-500 text-[10px] font-bold uppercase mb-1">Apreensão de Armas</p>
              <div className="flex items-center"><Crosshair className="text-orange-500 mr-2" size={20}/><span className="text-2xl font-bold">{totalArmas}</span></div>
              <p className="text-[9px] text-gray-400 mt-1">Ocorrências com armas</p>
            </button>
            <button onClick={() => setKpiFilter('drogas')} className={`bg-white p-4 rounded-xl shadow-sm border-l-4 flex flex-col justify-center text-left transition hover:scale-105 ${kpiFilter === 'drogas' ? 'border-red-500 ring-2 ring-red-200' : 'border-red-300'}`}>
              <p className="text-gray-500 text-[10px] font-bold uppercase mb-1">Apreensão Drogas</p>
              <div className="flex items-center"><AlertTriangle className="text-red-500 mr-2" size={20}/><span className="text-2xl font-bold">{totalDrogas}</span></div>
              <p className="text-[9px] text-gray-400 mt-1">Ocorrências com tráfico</p>
            </button>
            <button onClick={() => setKpiFilter('prisoes')} className={`bg-white p-4 rounded-xl shadow-sm border-l-4 flex flex-col justify-center text-left transition hover:scale-105 ${kpiFilter === 'prisoes' ? 'border-gray-800 ring-2 ring-gray-400' : 'border-gray-300'}`}>
              <p className="text-gray-500 text-[10px] font-bold uppercase mb-1">Prisões / Conduções</p>
              <div className="flex items-center"><Users className="text-gray-800 mr-2" size={20}/><span className="text-2xl font-bold">{totalPrisoes}</span></div>
              <p className="text-[9px] text-gray-400 mt-1">Pessoas Presas</p>
            </button>
            <button onClick={() => setKpiFilter('procedimentos')} className={`bg-white p-4 rounded-xl shadow-sm border-l-4 flex flex-col justify-center text-left transition hover:scale-105 ${kpiFilter === 'procedimentos' ? 'border-blue-600 ring-2 ring-blue-200' : 'border-blue-300'}`}>
              <p className="text-gray-500 text-[10px] font-bold uppercase mb-1">Procedimentos</p>
              <div className="flex items-center"><Gavel className="text-blue-600 mr-2" size={20}/><span className="text-2xl font-bold">{totalProcedimentos}</span></div>
              <p className="text-[9px] text-gray-400 mt-1">BO / TCO / APF</p>
            </button>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}

      <div className="bg-white p-4 rounded-xl shadow-sm border flex flex-wrap gap-4 items-end">
        <div>
          <label className="block text-xs font-bold text-gray-500 uppercase">Data Inicial</label>
          <input type="date" className="p-2 border rounded text-sm w-full" value={filterDataIni} onChange={e => setFilterDataIni(e.target.value)} />
        </div>
        <div>
          <label className="block text-xs font-bold text-gray-500 uppercase">Data Final</label>
          <input type="date" className="p-2 border rounded text-sm w-full" value={filterDataFim} onChange={e => setFilterDataFim(e.target.value)} />
        </div>
        <div className="flex-1 min-w-[200px]">
          <label className="block text-xs font-bold text-gray-500 uppercase">Buscar Natureza</label>
          <input type="text" placeholder="Ex: TRÁFICO..." className="p-2 border rounded text-sm w-full uppercase" value={filterNatureza} onChange={e => setFilterNatureza(e.target.value.toUpperCase())} />
        </div>
        {isGestor && (
          <div className="flex-1 min-w-[200px]">
            <label className="block text-xs font-bold text-gray-500 uppercase">Procurar PM</label>
            <input type="text" placeholder="Nome ou Matrícula..." className="p-2 border rounded text-sm w-full uppercase" value={filterPolicial} onChange={e => setFilterPolicial(e.target.value.toUpperCase())} />
          </div>
        )}
      </div>

      <div className="bg-indigo-50 border border-indigo-200 rounded-xl p-4 shadow-sm">
        <div className="flex flex-col md:flex-row md:items-center md:justify-between gap-3">
          <div>
            <h3 className="text-lg font-bold text-indigo-900">Georreferenciamento das ocorrências</h3>
            <p className="text-sm text-indigo-700">Os pontos abaixo são alimentados em tempo real com base no campo de latitude/longitude informado no ROP.</p>
          </div>
          <button onClick={() => setShowGeoMap(prev => !prev)} className="bg-white border border-indigo-300 text-indigo-900 px-4 py-2 rounded-lg text-sm font-bold shadow-sm hover:bg-indigo-100">
            {showGeoMap ? 'Ocultar mapa' : 'Mostrar mapa em tempo real'}
          </button>
        </div>

        <div className="mt-4 flex flex-wrap gap-3">
          <div className="bg-white border border-indigo-200 rounded-lg px-4 py-3">
            <span className="block text-[11px] uppercase font-bold text-indigo-700">Ocorrências filtradas</span>
            <strong className="text-2xl text-indigo-900">{filteredOcs.length}</strong>
          </div>
          <div className="bg-white border border-indigo-200 rounded-lg px-4 py-3">
            <span className="block text-[11px] uppercase font-bold text-indigo-700">Ocorrências com coordenadas</span>
            <strong className="text-2xl text-indigo-900">{ocorrenciasGeorreferenciadas.length}</strong>
          </div>
        </div>

        {showGeoMap && <div className="mt-4"><GeoOccurrenceAnalytics ocorrencias={filteredOcs} /></div>}
      </div>

      <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-3 gap-6">
        {filteredOcs.map(c => {
           const cmde = c.equipe?.[0];
           const hasApreensao = (c.armas && c.armas.length>2) || (c.entorpecentes && c.entorpecentes.length>2);

           return (
             <div key={c.id} className="bg-white rounded-xl shadow-md overflow-hidden border-t-4 border-indigo-700 relative">
               <div className="p-5">
                 <div className="flex justify-between items-start mb-2">
                   <div className="w-2/3">
                     <h3 className="text-lg font-bold text-indigo-900 truncate" title={c.natureza}>{c.natureza}</h3>
                     <p className="text-[10px] text-gray-500 uppercase font-bold">{c.municipio} • {c.procedimento}</p>
                     {c.mikeOcorrencia && <p className="text-[10px] text-indigo-700 font-bold uppercase">Mike: {c.mikeOcorrencia}</p>}
                   </div>
                   <div className="text-right w-1/3">
                     <span className="text-xs text-gray-800 font-bold block">{c.dataOcorrencia ? c.dataOcorrencia.split('-').reverse().join('/') : '--'}</span>
                     <span className="text-[10px] text-gray-500">{c.horaInicial} • {c.duracaoOcorrenciaLabel || 'sem duração'}</span>
                   </div>
                 </div>
                 
                 <div className="my-3 bg-gray-50 p-2 rounded border border-gray-100">
                   <p className="text-gray-800 text-xs font-bold truncate">CMDE: {cmde?.posto} {cmde?.nome}</p>
                   <p className="text-gray-500 text-[10px] truncate" title={c.local}>Local: {c.local}</p>
                 </div>

                 {hasApreensao && <span className="text-[9px] bg-red-100 text-red-800 px-2 py-0.5 rounded font-bold uppercase inline-block mb-1 border border-red-200">Com Apreensões Relevantes</span>}
                 {(c.coordenadasGeograficas || parseCoordinates(c.coordenadas)) && <span className="text-[9px] bg-indigo-100 text-indigo-800 px-2 py-0.5 rounded font-bold uppercase inline-block mb-1 ml-1 border border-indigo-200">Mapeada</span>}
               </div>
               <div className="bg-gray-50 p-3 border-t flex justify-end space-x-2 items-center">
                  {isDev && (
                    <button onClick={() => { if(window.confirm('Apagar Ocorrência permanentemente?')) onDelete(c.id) }} className="text-red-500 hover:bg-red-100 p-1.5 rounded mr-auto" title="Apagar">
                      <Trash2 size={16}/>
                    </button>
                  )}
                  <button onClick={() => setViewOcorrencia(c)} className="text-sm flex items-center bg-white border border-gray-300 px-3 py-1 rounded hover:bg-gray-100 shadow-sm font-semibold text-indigo-900">
                    <Eye size={14} className="mr-1"/> Detalhes
                  </button>
                  <button onClick={() => setPrintLayout({ type: 'ocorrencia', data: c })} className="text-sm flex items-center bg-indigo-900 text-white px-3 py-1 rounded hover:bg-indigo-800 shadow-sm font-semibold">
                    <Printer size={14} className="mr-1"/> Imprimir ROP
                  </button>
               </div>
             </div>
           )
        })}
        {filteredOcs.length === 0 && <p className="text-gray-500">Nenhuma ocorrência encontrada.</p>}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

function OcorrenciaModal({ data, onClose, isDev, onDelete }) {
  if (!data) return null;

  return (
    <div className="fixed inset-0 bg-black bg-opacity-70 flex items-center justify-center z-50 p-4 pt-10 pb-10">
      <div className="bg-white rounded-xl shadow-2xl w-full max-w-4xl h-full flex flex-col overflow-hidden animate-fadeIn">
        <div className="bg-indigo-900 text-white p-4 flex justify-between items-center">
          <h2 className="font-bold text-lg flex items-center"><ClipboardList className="mr-2"/> ROP - {data.natureza}</h2>
          <div className="flex space-x-3">
            {isDev && <button onClick={() => { if(window.confirm('Apagar?')) onDelete(data.id) }} className="hover:bg-red-600 bg-red-500 p-1.5 rounded transition shadow-sm text-white"><Trash2 size={18}/></button>}
            <button onClick={onClose} className="hover:bg-indigo-800 p-1.5 rounded transition"><XCircle size={24}/></button>
          </div>
        </div>
        
        <div className="p-6 overflow-y-auto flex-1 space-y-6 text-sm">
          
          <div className="grid grid-cols-2 md:grid-cols-6 gap-4 bg-gray-50 p-4 rounded-lg border">
            <div><span className="block text-xs text-gray-500 uppercase">01. Data</span><strong className="text-gray-800">{data.dataOcorrencia?.split('-').reverse().join('/')}</strong></div>
            <div><span className="block text-xs text-gray-500 uppercase">02/03. Horário</span><strong className="text-gray-800">{data.horaInicial} às {data.horaFinal}</strong></div>
            <div><span className="block text-xs text-gray-500 uppercase">04. Turno</span><strong className="text-gray-800">{data.turno}</strong></div>
            <div><span className="block text-xs text-gray-500 uppercase">Supervisor</span><strong className="text-gray-800">{data.supervisor || 'N/I'}</strong></div>
            <div><span className="block text-xs text-gray-500 uppercase">MIKE DA OCORRÊNCIA</span><strong className="text-gray-800">{data.mikeOcorrencia || 'N/I'}</strong></div>
            <div><span className="block text-xs text-gray-500 uppercase">07. Município</span><strong className="text-gray-800">{data.municipio}</strong></div>
            
            <div className="md:col-span-3"><span className="block text-xs text-gray-500 uppercase">05. Local</span><strong className="text-gray-800">{data.local}</strong></div>
            <div className="md:col-span-3">
              <span className="block text-xs text-gray-500 uppercase">06. Coordenadas</span>
              <strong className="text-gray-800">{data.coordenadas || 'N/I'}</strong>
              {(data.coordenadasGeograficas || parseCoordinates(data.coordenadas)) && (
                <a
                  href={`https://www.google.com/maps?q=${(data.coordenadasGeograficas || parseCoordinates(data.coordenadas)).lat},${(data.coordenadasGeograficas || parseCoordinates(data.coordenadas)).lng}`}
                  target="_blank"
                  rel="noreferrer"
                  className="block text-xs font-bold text-indigo-700 mt-1"
                >
                  Abrir ponto no mapa
                </a>
              )}
            </div>
            
            <div><span className="block text-xs text-gray-500 uppercase">08. Tipo Policiamento</span><strong className="text-gray-800">{data.tipoPoliciamento}</strong></div>
            <div><span className="block text-xs text-gray-500 uppercase">09. VTR</span><strong className="text-gray-800">{data.prefixo || 'N/I'}</strong></div>
            <div className="md:col-span-4"><span className="block text-xs text-gray-500 uppercase">10. HT / 15. Apoio</span><strong className="text-gray-800">HT: {data.ht || '-'} | Apoio: {data.apoio || '-'}</strong></div>
            
            <div><span className="block text-xs text-gray-500 uppercase">OPM</span><strong className="text-gray-800">{data.opm || 'N/I'}</strong></div>
            <div className="md:col-span-5"><span className="block text-xs text-gray-500 uppercase">Área de Atuação</span><strong className="text-gray-800">{data.areaAtuacao || 'N/I'}</strong></div>
          </div>

          <div className="bg-blue-50 p-4 rounded-lg border border-blue-200">
             <h3 className="font-bold text-blue-900 mb-2 uppercase border-b border-blue-200 pb-1">Composição da Equipe (11 a 14)</h3>
             <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 gap-2">
                {(data.equipe || []).map((eq, i) => {
                  if(!eq.matricula) return null;
                  return (
                    <div key={i} className="bg-white p-2 rounded border border-blue-100 flex justify-between items-center">
                      <div>
                        <span className="text-[10px] text-blue-600 font-bold block">{eq.funcao}</span>
                        <span className="font-bold text-gray-800 text-xs">{eq.posto} {eq.nomeCompleto || eq.nome}</span>
                      </div>
                      <span className="text-[10px] text-gray-500 font-mono">Mat: {eq.matricula}</span>
                    </div>
                  )
                })}
             </div>
          </div>

          <div>
             <h3 className="font-bold text-lg border-b pb-1 mb-3 text-gray-800">17. Narrativa da Ocorrência</h3>
             <div className="bg-gray-50 p-4 rounded border text-gray-700 text-justify whitespace-pre-wrap leading-relaxed">
               {data.narrativa}
             </div>
          </div>

          <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 gap-4">
             <div className="bg-orange-50 p-4 rounded border border-orange-200">
               <h4 className="font-bold text-orange-900 mb-2 border-b border-orange-200 pb-1">Apreensões</h4>
               <ul className="text-sm space-y-2">
                 <li><strong className="text-orange-800">18. Material:</strong> {data.materialApresentado || '-'}</li>
                 <li><strong className="text-orange-800">19. Veículos:</strong> {data.veiculos || '-'}</li>
                 <li><strong className="text-orange-800">20. Armas:</strong> {data.armas || '-'}</li>
                 <li><strong className="text-orange-800">21. Drogas:</strong> {data.entorpecentes || '-'}</li>
